互联网技术/架构/团队

CentOS添加路由表-支持双网卡双网关

2016-08-12 linux linux 双网卡 路由

 如果在rc.local中添加路由会造成NFS无法自动挂载问题，所以使用static-routes的方法是最好的。无论重启系统和service network restart 都会生效。

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;按照linux启动的顺序，rc.local里面的内容是在linux所有服务都启动完毕，最后才被执行的，也就是说，这里面的内容是在netfs之后才被执行的，那也就是说在netfs启动的时候，服务器上的静态路由是没有被添加的，所以netfs挂载不能成功。static-routes文件又是什么呢，这个是network脚本执行时调用的一个文件。</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">如果你重启了服务器，那么路由就失效了，这个时候你不得不重新加载这个文件，但是如果你是远程操作的呢？所以，这个方法是非常的不推荐.</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;如果系统只是做网络连接应用，也是可以用的。</span></span>

<span style="line-height: 1.6; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, serif; font-size: 14px;">环境：centos6.6系统已经验证，</span>

<span style="line-height: 1.6; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, serif; font-size: 14px;">一台主机两块网卡，两个IP地址，</span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;(外网)</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">172.172.20.62&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 255.255.254.0&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 172.172.21.254</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;（内网）</span></span>

59.201.201.173&nbsp; 255.255.255.0&nbsp;&nbsp; 59.201.201.254

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;开启ip转发(永久开启)</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">vi /etc/sysctl.conf&nbsp; -----net.ipv4.ip_forward=1&nbsp;</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;#sysctl -p</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">方案一：</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">一、设置ip</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">为网卡eth1配置ip地址----(内网)-不设置网关</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">vi /etc/sysconfig/network-scripts/ifcfg-eth1</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;二、编辑路由表</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">修改vi&nbsp;/etc/iproute2/rt_tables，末尾添加内容：</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">252 &nbsp; net59</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">251 &nbsp; net172</span></span>

&nbsp;

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">#在vi&nbsp;/etc/rc.local里添加原路返回路由</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;vi&nbsp;/etc/rc.d/rc.local</span></span>

##

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip&nbsp;route&nbsp;flush table net59</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip route add default via 59.201.201.254 dev eth1 src 59.201.201.173 table net59</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip rule add from 59.201.201.173 table net59</span></span>

&nbsp;

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip route flush table net172</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip route add default via 172.172.21.254 dev eth2 src&nbsp;172.172.20.62&nbsp;table net172</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">ip rule add from&nbsp;172.172.20.62&nbsp;table net172</span></span>

#

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">如果重启网卡，一定要带上/etc/rc.d/rc.local</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">service network restart&nbsp;&amp;&amp;&nbsp;/etc/rc.d/rc.local</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">查看路由：</span></span>

<span style="font-size: 14px;"><span style="font-family: times new roman,times,serif;">route -n</span></span>
